            PsiElement(Perl5 POD: code)(' #!/usr/bin/perl -Tw\n use strict;\n BEGIN { $ENV{PATH} = "/usr/bin:/bin" }\n use Socket;\n use Carp;\n my $EOL = "\015\012";\n\n sub spawn;  # forward declaration\n sub logmsg { print "$0 $$: @_ at ", scalar localtime(), "\n" }\n\n my $port  = shift || 2345;\n die "invalid port" unless $port =~ /^ \d+ $/x;\n\n my $proto = getprotobyname("tcp");\n\n socket(Server, PF_INET, SOCK_STREAM, $proto)   || die "socket: $!";\n setsockopt(Server, SOL_SOCKET, SO_REUSEADDR, pack("l", 1))\n                                                || die "setsockopt: $!";\n bind(Server, sockaddr_in($port, INADDR_ANY))   || die "bind: $!";\n listen(Server, SOMAXCONN)                      || die "listen: $!";\n\n logmsg "server started on port $port";\n\n my $waitedpid = 0;\n my $paddr;\n\n use POSIX ":sys_wait_h";\n use Errno;\n\n sub REAPER {\n     local $!;   # don't let waitpid() overwrite current error\n     while ((my $pid = waitpid(-1, WNOHANG)) > 0 && WIFEXITED($?)) {\n         logmsg "reaped $waitedpid" . ($? ? " with exit $?" : "");\n     }\n     $SIG{CHLD} = \&REAPER;  # loathe SysV\n }\n\n $SIG{CHLD} = \&REAPER;\n\n while (1) {\n     $paddr = accept(Client, Server) || do {\n         # try again if accept() returned because got a signal\n         next if $!{EINTR};\n         die "accept: $!";\n     };\n     my ($port, $iaddr) = sockaddr_in($paddr);\n     my $name = gethostbyaddr($iaddr, AF_INET);\n\n     logmsg "connection from $name [",\n            inet_ntoa($iaddr),\n            "] at port $port";\n\n     spawn sub {\n         $| = 1;\n         print "Hello there, $name, it's now ",\n               scalar localtime(),\n               $EOL;\n         exec "/usr/games/fortune"       # XXX: "wrong" line terminators\n             or confess "can't exec fortune: $!";\n     };\n     close Client;\n }\n\n sub spawn {\n     my $coderef = shift;\n\n     unless (@_ == 0 && $coderef && ref($coderef) eq "CODE") {\n         confess "usage: spawn CODEREF";\n     }\n\n     my $pid;\n     unless (defined($pid = fork())) {\n         logmsg "cannot fork: $!";\n         return;\n     }\n     elsif ($pid) {\n         logmsg "begat $pid";\n         return; # I'm the parent\n     }\n     # else I'm the child -- go spawn\n\n     open(STDIN,  "<&Client")    || die "can't dup client to stdin";\n     open(STDOUT, ">&Client")    || die "can't dup client to stdout";\n     ## open(STDERR, ">&STDOUT") || die "can't dup stdout to stderr";\n     exit($coderef->());\n }\n')

($? ? " with exit $?" : "");\n        }\n        $SIG{CHLD} = \&REAPER;  # loathe SysV\n    }\n\n    $SIG{CHLD} = \&REAPER;\n\n\n    for ( $waitedpid = 0;\n          accept(Client, Server) || $waitedpid;\n          $waitedpid = 0, close Client)\n    {\n        next if $waitedpid;\n        logmsg "connection on $NAME";\n        spawn sub {\n            print "Hello there, it's now ", scalar localtime(), "\n";\n            exec("/usr/games/fortune")  || die "can't exec fortune: $!";\n        };\n    }\n\n    sub spawn {\n        my $coderef = shift();\n\n        unless (@_ == 0 && $coderef && ref($coderef) eq "CODE") {\n            confess "usage: spawn CODEREF";\n        }\n\n        my $pid;\n        unless (defined($pid = fork())) {\n            logmsg "cannot fork: $!";\n            return;\n        }\n        elsif ($pid) {\n            logmsg "begat $pid";\n            return; # I'm the parent\n        }\n        else {\n            # I'm the child -- go spawn\n        }\n\n        open(STDIN,  "<&Client")    || die "can't dup client to stdin";\n        open(STDOUT, ">&Client")    || die "can't dup client to stdout";\n        ## open(STDERR, ">&STDOUT") || die "can't dup stdout to stderr";\n        exit($coderef->());\n    }\n')
